 google ne is maukey par ek khaas doodle banaaya he or unki tasviir se saath GOOGLE likhaa gaya he
 v Shantaram's original name was Rajaram Vankurde Shantaram
 cinema kii duniya main unhen aise filmkaar ke rup main yaad kiya jaataa he, jinhone saamaajik or paariwarik prishthbhumi par arthpurna filmein banaakar lagbhag chah dashakon tak darshakon ke dil main raaj kiya
 He was born on 18 November 1901 in Kolhapur, Maharashtra
 400 saal purana he kedarnath mandir kaa itihaas, khaas pattharon se hua nirmanjane unke bare main 
 
 
 
 
 At the time when the Hindi film industry was in its early stages of development, there was also a filmmaker who used 'do Aankhen Barah Haath', 'dr
 Aankhen Barah Haath', in camera, screenplay, acting and technique
 kotnis kii amar kahani', 'jhanak jhanak paayal baaje' or 'navrang' jaisi kai bemisaal filmein banaai
 Shantaram, who has given many social films in Hindi and Marathi languages in the long film journey, did not get education, but his films are textbooks for the students of film cinema
 shantaram kaa rujhaan shuru se hi filmon kii ore tha
 He wanted to become a filmmaker
 filmon main kariyar banane kii shuruyaat main unhone gandharva naatak mandali main chhot-mote kaam karne se kii
 It is said that the father of the film world is V
 shantaram gandharva naatak mandali main pardaa uthaane kaa kaam kiya karte the
 He later joined Baburao Painter's Maharashtra Film Company, where he got the finer details of film production
 haalanki us dauraan painter ne unhen abhinay ke liye choti-choti bhoomikaayen bhi deen
 This finance minister of India had become the first Prime Minister of Pakistan to tell that the era was of silent films
 shantaram ne 1927 main netaji paalkar kaa nirdesan kiya
 He later founded the Prabhat Film Company with three-four people
 shuru main ve painter se kaaphi prabhavit rahe or unheen kii tarah puranic or aitihaasik filmein banaate rahe
 It is said of him that he once went to Germany, where his cinematic vision got a new direction
 uske baad unhone gambhir or saamaajik filmon kii taraf rukh kiya
 During this time he made films like 'duniya na mane aadmi', 'neighbor' etc
 ye baat saal 1942 kii he jab prabhaat company ke partner alag hokar shantaram ne usee saal raajakmal kalamandir kii sthapana kii
 From here he began a new and spectacular phase which continued for the next several decades
 us dauraan unhone kai behtareen filmein banaai
 These films include 'shakuntala', 'amar Kahani of Dr
 Kotnis', 'jeevan Yatra', 'jhank Jhank Payal Baje', 'navrang', 'sehra', Jal Bin fish-dance Bin Bijli, Two Eyes Twelve Hands etc
 
 google doodle par chai duniya kii sabase khubasurat mahiladada sahab phalke puraskaar or padam vibhushanshantharam kaa safar maan-sammaan bharaa rahaa
 In 1985, in view of his contribution to the film world, he was awarded the Dadasaheb Phalke Award and Padma Vibhushan Award, the highest honor of the film industry in India
 chah dashak ke filmi safar main unhone aisi filmein banaai jo amar ho gai

 Political background The first election in Hoshangabad Lok Sabha seat was held in 1951
 is chunaav main congress ke saiyad ahamed ne nirdaleey ummidavaar rahe echvi kamath ko haraaya tha
 However, in the by-elections held here in 1952, Syed Ahmed lost to HV Kamath
 1957 main congress ne yahaan par vaapasi kii or 1958 ke upachunaav main bhi jeet hasil kii
 In 1962, the Congress once faced defeat here
 1962 kaa chunaav haarane ke baad congress 1967 main ek baar phir vaapasi kii or daulat singh yahaan ke saansad bane
 BJP won this seat for the first time in the 1989 election
 sartaaj singh ne congress kii ore se do baar saansad rahe rameshwar nakhra ko haraaya
 Sartaj Singh also won the 1991, 1996 and 1998 elections thereafter
 1999 main bijepi ne rajya ke purv siem sunderlaal patwa ko tikat diya or unhone congress ke rajkumaar patel ko kareeb 50 hajaar voton se maat de di
 In the 2004 elections, Sartaj was again fielded by BJP and Sartaj Singh did not disappoint his party
 unhone congress ke omprakash hajarilal ko shikast di

 2009 kaa chunaav congress ke tikat par ladane vaale udai pratap singh ne 2014 main bijepi ke tikat par ladate hue jeet hasil kii

 " singh ke anusaar, "supreme court ne saafe kaha he giraftaar us vaqt kii jaani chahie jab jaanch kii disha na mil paae or aaropee jaanch main sahyog na kare lekin aseem ke maamle main ye donon hi sahi nahin baithte hai

 The police will have to tell in the court whether the cartoon of Aseem has created a sense of rebellion in the country
 
 
 kya aseem ke cartoon ko kisi sajeesh ke tahat banaakar logon ko dikhaaya gaya he
 
 
 Has anyone revolted against the government after seeing Asim's cartoon? jaankaar ab yah sawaal bhi uthaa rahe hai ki jab police ko aseem kii hiraasat nahin chahie thi to tab ravivaar ko peshi ke dauraan aseem kii hiraasat kii maang hi kyon kii gai
 Legal expert Ashish Chavan told, "I have not seen such a case in my career so far when the police first asks for custody and then surrenders it the very next day
 yah police kii manshaa bataati he kii vah cese ko lekar kis tarah kaam kar rahi he
 " ab jabaki aseem kaa kahana he ki vah maamle kii sunwaayee ke liye na to vakil kii seva legaa or na hi jamaanat to aise main aseem ke jail se bahaar aane ke sirf gine-chune vikalp hi bachate hai
 According to Chavan, "if the police wants, then by filing a petition under section 169, Aseem can demand the dismissal of the case and by not opposing Aseem's bail, he can also help in giving bail to Aseem

 "tippaniyan On the other hand, Aseem's troubles have not diminished
 agar sarkaar chaahe to bhi maamle ko khatm nahin kar sakati he, kyonki maamle ke shikayatakarta ke paas police kii jaanch ke khilaaf aawaaj uthaane kaa puraa haq hota he or vah maamle kii phir se jaanch kii maang ke saath-saath jaanch kisi or agency se karaane kii darkhwaast kar sakati he
 However, sedition cases have been registered against Aseem not only in Mumbai but also in Maharashtra's Beed district

 Police told the court that apart from Aseem, they are looking for more people who helped Aseem to make cartoons and upload them on the Internet
 kanoonee jaankaar aseem kii hiraasat par sawaal uthaa rahe hai
 Former IPS YP Singh says, "if the magistrate's order has also come to the police, then the police would continue to register the case and investigate, but the arrest of the Supreme Court has been disregarded
" " According to Singh, "the Supreme Court has clearly said that the arrest should be made when the direction of investigation is not found and the accused does not cooperate in the investigation, but in the case of Aseem, both of them do not fit
" " Knowing the legalities, they say that Aseem has been arrested, but even if the police wants, the matter cannot be brought for hearing in the court

 "comments duusari ore, aseem kii mushkilen kam nahin hui hai
